[30;1m115 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m116 | [0m[35mDetermining that a feed is password-protected[0m
[30;1m117 | [0m[35m---------------------------------------------[0m
[30;1m118 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m119 | [0m[35m::[0m

[31m--[ [0m[34mMatch #[0m[33m65[0m[34m of [0m[33m414[0m[31m ]--[0m
   Rule Id: [34mBD000701[0m
       Tag: [34mSecurity.Backdoor.DataExfiltration.Token[0m
  Severity: [36mImportant[0m, Confidence: [36mHigh[0m
  Filename: [33m/feedparser-6.0.11/docs/http-authentication.rst[0m
   Pattern: [32m(npm owner|password|htpasswd|auth_?token|secret_?key|private_?key|authorized_keys?|npmrc|\.ssh|usersecrets?|api_?keys|nuget\.config|\.identityservice)[0m
[30;1m108 | [0m[35myou will need to parse it yourself.  Everything before the first space is the[0m
[30;1m109 | [0m[35mtype of authentication (probably ``Basic`` or ``Digest``), which controls which[0m
[30;1m110 | [0m[35mtype of handler you'll need to construct.  The realm name is given as[0m
[30;1m111 | [0m[35mrealm="foo" -- so foo would be your first argument to auth.add_password.  Other[0m
[30;1m112 | [0m[35minformation in the www-authenticate header is probably safe to ignore; the[0m
[30;1m113 | [0m[35m:file:`urllib2` module will handle it for you.[0m
[30;1m114 | [0m[35m[0m

[31m--[ [0m[34mMatch #[0m[33m66[0m[34m of [0m[33m414[0m[31m ]--[0m

  Filename: [33m/feedparser-6.0.11/docs/http-authentication.rst[0m
   Pattern: [32m(npm owner|password|htpasswd|auth_?token|secret_?key|private_?key|authorized_keys?|npmrc|\.ssh|usersecrets?|api_?keys|nuget\.config|\.identityservice)[0m
[30;1m98 | [0m[35mpassword-protected.  But what if you don't know?[0m
[30;1m99 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m100 | [0m[35mIf you try to download a password-protected feed without sending all the proper[0m
[30;1m101 | [0m[35mpassword information, the server will return an [0m
[30;1m102 | [0m[35m:abbr:`HTTP (Hypertext Transfer Protocol)` status code ``401``.[0m
[30;1m103 | [0m[35m:program:`Universal Feed Parser` makes this status code available in[0m
[30;1m104 | [0m[35m``d.status``.[0m

[30;1m97 | [0m[35mThe examples so far have assumed that you know in advance that the feed is[0m

[30;1m85 | [0m[35m        realm = re.findall('realm="([^"]*)"', headers['WWW-Authenticate'])[0][0m
[30;1m86 | [0m[35m        self.add_password(realm, host, user, passw)[0m
[30;1m87 | [0m[35m        retry = self.http_error_auth_reqed('www-authenticate', host, req, headers)[0m
[30;1m88 | [0m[35m        self.reset_retry_count()[0m
[30;1m89 | [0m[35m        return retry[0m
